<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
My friend suggested we try El Salvadoran tamales and oh what a wonderful experience! We sat outside. The place was full of people who seemed to be Salvadoran, a very good sign.

The lady I assume to be Xina was warm, calm, kind, and unflappable. She made me feel like her only customer while the room was packed with people.

Sitting in the sun outside to eat the tamales, she served us in the same manner as inside, warm, calm, kind, and unflappable. And the tamales were beyond incredible! I'm already hooked on Mexican tamales. These were entirely different in texture, seasoning and in taste and they were fabulous. The vegetable was mixed into the masa harina dough and the beans were a paste inside. Sorry those of you used to this presentation thinking, "Duh!", but it was all new and exciting for me. The price is right too. Where are 10 stars when you need them?< /text>

<user_name>Anne Hartman< /user_name><Date>1436761078671<//Date><rate>1< /rate>< Review>
I was extremely disappointed with Foothill Boarding Kennel. I dropped my dog off at the kennel the day of our vacation and was called 5:30 pm that same day, when I was already out of the state, and was told that I needed to have someone come pick up my dog! My dog was kicked out of the kennel!!! I have not heard of that ever happening to anyone. They claimed he tried to bite someone. Although, he didn't bite anyone and has not bitten anyone before. He is a 60 lb. dog who does jump.This is an established kennel and I have always known it to exist the last 20 years I have visited and lived in Oroville. I guess it was wrong of me to think the employees know how to care for dogs. My dog doesn't have a lot of experience at kennels and does have some anxiety, but has been in the care of other people and has not had any problems. I was upfront about my dog's nervousness, and was asked when I checked him in if he would be ok. I was certain he would be ok, but said it may take a little time getting used to the new situation. It was very upsetting getting a call that other arrangements needed to be made for my dog. If I had other arrangements I wouldn't have needed the kennel. What a stressful way to start vacation. Thankfully,I was able to get my dog taken to another kennel in the area and he had a wonderful experience.< /Review>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures><response>None< /response>< Review>
This is a single star of bitterness.

I used to eat at the Green Chile in the city when it started because it was a block from my friend's apartment, and became our hung over breakfast burrito spot. Over the years I have watched it become more and more popular, but also more and more expensive. The food is good, and the ingredients are high quality, but if you are looking for a good burrito, there are other places in Marin.

Unfortunately, as of today I will officially never eat here again. I went to the San Rafael location for a burrito (steak, sour cream, guac) after a long Green Chile hiatus, and they charged me a shocking $20+, with no drink. The Bay is expensive, but that is just a Marin gringo rip off. This food, though it is tasty, is simply not worth the price tag. Some restaurants open in Marin just thinking that because people in the area might have money, they can charge whatever they want. This is how a lot of places go out of business around here, because in reality people are tight with their money, and if the value isn't there, they go elsewhere... I've seen it a lot growing up. Anyway, boo hoo, but I would suggest Picante in the Canal, or Mi Pueblo in San Anselmo.</Review>

<Date>1403708350815<//Date><rate>4< /rate><review>This is considered the "Beverly Hills" location.  There's nothing Beverly Hills about it.  It's run down, equipment is old, it's not very well lit, it smells a bit, and is literally located in the basement of an office building.

The weight room and a basketball court were closed down because a pipe burst and flooded the place.  That was probably the best thing that could have happened!  It forced me to go to the Ocean Park location and the Hollywood location.  Those are AMAZING! They provide you with towels, the staff is friendly, they smell nice, and have new equipment.  That is probably why EVERYONE and their mom goes there! If waiting in line to use any type of equipment, those are the places for you!

When this location opened back up, I realized how great it really is!  I can literally walk in, and start working out immediately and not have to worry about waiting to use any equipment there.  Even when it's busy, it's not that busy.  All the disadvantages of this place actually work to your advantage if all you really care about is working out!

Lily Yip<//Name>
< time>
1417934868187<//time>
<Rating>2<//Rating>< Review>
This gym is literally "the dungeon."

For the first-timers who've never been here before, this gym is "hidden" within the parking structure/plaza that has a cafe. Just follow the 24 Hour Fitness sign, and walk down the stairs. You'll see an elevator or stairs to go to the basement and that's where the gym is located.

This place doesn't have much ventilation. I usually come late at night or during the weekends so it's not too crowded.

As for parking, you can park at the meters for free before 7am or after 6pm. I'm definitely not going to park in the garage and pay for parking. That's just absurd.

The only reason why I go here is because it's the closest one to where I live. If I had a choice, I would go to another 24 gym that's bigger and cleaner.

FYI, this place is not 24/7. The hours are misleading. They actually close at 11pm on Fridays, and open 5am-11pm on Sat/Sun.<//Review>

< review>
The pizza was really good. I got the King Arthur special, it's loaded with toppings. Once the order was in it took at least 25 minutes to get our pizza. They make their pizza when you place your order and that's why it takes a little longer and they thoroughly cook it. They use quality toppings and cheeses. I guess because this location is walking distance to the beach their rent is expensive and it shows in the price of the pizza. I got a small King Arthur special (8 small slices) and it cost $17 but compared to the $7 chocolate shake I got from a lunch truck/ice cream truck that was parked by the beach it's not too over-priced. <pictures>None<//pictures>< text>
I was a patient of Dr. Valenton (who I loved) until I got pregnant. She wasn't able to take on new OBs, which I was really disappointed about. My first prenatal with another doctor there was horrible and in no way validating or helpful. In fact, I left with more questions and uncertainty than before. The ultrasound experience left me feeling helpless. Throughout the entire visit, I was told not to be upset, not to cry, and that I had the wrong attitude. This all after I was informed that the embryo was measuring small (which from prior research and friends' experiences translates to increased likelihood of miscarriage). I was told there was "nothing we can do" and that "we don't know anything yet"...so naturally, my heart sank and I felt really scared and disappointed. When I started expressing those emotions--by myself, mind you, because my partner wasn't allowed to be with me due to COVID--the doctor then somewhat scolded me for reacting that way.

In an attempt (maybe?) to offer me something, she encouraged bloodwork for genetic testing for both me and my partner. Magically, he was able to come in then! At this point, I had been congratulated by office staff and the lab tech (which felt strange to me because 1) I wasn't feeling very optimistic and hearing that made me even sadder, and 2) what if this was not a wanted pregnancy at all and these people were making me feel guilty for wanting to choose differently...).

In the end, it was not a good appointment. I did not walk away having any real sense of what was going on with my body. I had to go home and call friends and look online (which is NEVER a fun time). I felt helpless and hopeless, and the professionals in charge really let my partner and me down. Needless to say, I found another women's health group today and in one phone call, I already feel better. If this little embryo doesn't miscarry by next week, we will hopefully be in better hands.</text>

After spending years dealing with extreme uterine cramps and pain that caused me to miss 2-4 days per month from work for almost 10 years as well as severe anemia, my friend referred me to Dr. Stacey Rosenbaum, who was amazing!  Very relatable, vibrant, positive and a clear communicator.  I ended up having a much-needed myomectomy to remove several fibroids/adenomyomas and I ended up healing quickly with Dr. Rosenbaum as the surgeon.  Shortly after my surgery, Dr. Rosenbaum took a personal leave and I was bummed.  Where would I find another great, honest, vibrant, skilled and positive GYN DR who was also a great communicator?  Well, enter Dr. Rebecca Brown.  Dr. Stacey referred me to her... and I was hesitant.  Would she be just as great as Dr. Rosenbaum?  The answer is YES.  Dr. Rebecca Brown grabbed the baton from Dr. Stacey, assured me that I was in good hands and took over as my doctor.  I eventually had a partial hysterectomy and Dr. Rebecca Brown made the whole process smooth and easy... She is pleasant, patient and extremely skilled.  The healing with this surgery was obviously tougher than the previous procedure, but I managed my expectations after Dr. Brown walked me through every detailed step.  I also healed very quickly... faster than expected... due to Dr. Brown's skill.  I am grateful to Dr. Brown... as well as Rodeo Drive Women's Health Center for having such a supportive staff of doctors, nurses, receptionists...
